msg:The hotel is a new hotel that opened last year, and all kinds of facilities are brand new. We booked this hotel for a concert, but we didn't expect to have an unexpected surprise. The hotel is located on the bank of Qiantang River, overlooking the magnificent scenery of Qiantang River every day, which is refreshing. The front desk and other staff are friendly. The hotel seems to be located in Hangzhou New District, but the transportation is very convenient. It takes four stops from the hotel to reach the West Lake Scenic Area on Metro Line 1 (it takes about ten minutes to walk from the hotel to the Metro Station on Line 1). Hangzhou's bus and subway connections are very good, so don't worry about being far from West Lake and inconvenient to travel. The breakfast dishes are rich and taste good. It takes only half an hour to take a taxi from the airport to Xiaoshan Airport. Friends who have the habit of road running every day can choose here. It's really cool to run by the Qiantang River! It's a pity that I didn't take pictures of the internal facilities of the hotel. The rooms are great! After all, it's newly opened.

msg:The service is very good + the facilities are very new and very good
Let’s talk about the service first. It’s my first time in Hangzhou.
Let’s talk about service first. When we arrived at the hotel lobby, the staff took the initiative to help us with our luggage. From the lobby to the front desk, their attitude was very, very good. They were very energetic and had a good image. When I checked in, they asked me if I had any ideas or requirements for the room, and they gave me Breakfast and welcome fruits were given. After checking in at night, I found that the air conditioner was running warm air because the temperature in Hangzhou has heated up in the past few days. After contacting the front desk, the staff was very considerate and sent a fan and turned the air conditioner in the room back to cold air. Thank you very much. When I came back from my trip the next day, I was very surprised to find that the clothes on the bed were all neatly folded, coats were hung, towels were changed, and mineral water was replenished. This gave FD and HSKP great praise.
As for the facilities, I stayed in room 1306. It has a great view and faces the river. The facilities are very new and easy to use. The air conditioner has low noise and the lights are comfortable. There are many charging sockets. The bathroom is separated from wet and dry. The design is very good. There is no odor from the bathroom to the room. The smell is quite pleasant.
It is highly recommended to stay here. I will stay here again next time I come to Hangzhou!
Fabulous stay, Amazing Front Desk & Housekeeping service.
First time in Hangzhou, lobby staff went out and help with the luggage when getting off taxi. Front desk comes up with big warm welcome and fabulous attitude, they do ask our room preference and giving free breakfast as well. After check in 10mins late the welcome fruit was sent to us as well. Big thanks for the team.

Thanks again for the great service from Front Desk and Housekeeping.

The shortcoming of the guest room is that the curtains of the two windows in the bedroom are opened in conjunction. They have to be opened and closed together. However, the shortcomings do not affect my overall satisfaction with the room.
    The hotel's configuration of the executive lounge is a bit random. Almost all the high-end hotels I have stayed in have executive lounges that are more particular about either good views or good decoration. Crown's executive lounge needs to improve its service awareness. The lounge is in the gym on the fourth floor. On the side, there is a strong smell of swimming pool disinfectant water, there is basically no scenery to speak of, and the decoration inside is like a university cafeteria. Except for the happy hour food in the evening, the afternoon tea is really simple. It's the Spring Festival, so there are a lot of people at the hotel for breakfast, and you almost have to wait in line after 8 o'clock. In this case, I hope the hotel can open an executive lounge to divert some people, so that guests who don't like too much excitement can have a relatively quiet dining environment. (Those who are not interested in administrative courtesy can ignore the above)

Environment: The hotel as a whole is in a modern and simple style. The lobby design is artistic, fresh and natural, and is suitable for both business and leisure. The hotel is located by the river, very close to the Asian Games Lotus Stadium, more than 2 kilometers away in a straight line, surrounded by green trees and lawns, and the air is pleasant.
Service: The staff is serious and responsible, the service is considerate and thoughtful, and check-in and check-out are very fast. In particular, the hotel received guests with great sincerity and gave us a surprising discount. It upgraded us to a river view room for free (the view is excellent, you can see the river view, the bridge and the Lotus Stadium from the room), and also gave us double copies for two days. Breakfast makes a great impression!
A little suggestion: The hotel's deposit policy is not clearly marked. When placing the order and booking, Ctrip collected a deposit of the full room rate. This condition was stated on Ctrip's website. However, when checking in, the hotel collected a deposit in excess of the room rate, which was not stated at the time of booking. I hope it will be clearly marked in the future.

msg:來看亞運的，總體來説還可以。但缺點也很明顯。
先説優點，地理位置非常優越，離錢塘江和奧體很近。房間景緻也不錯。
前台小姐姐服務很好，主動給升級了房間，點贊！
缺點在於，房間略小，衞生間水池設施設計不合理且水龍頭鬆動。除了前台小姐姐其餘人服務意識略有不足。早餐的標準有待提高。整體入住感覺衹能達到四星級酒店的標準。能理解國慶期間漲價，但是一千八的價格，體驗感不如在蘇州常住的洲際和南京的一些酒店。性價比有待提高。

btw，張經理聲音很好聽，必是人美心善，魅力十足。

生日期間入住的本以為會有小驚喜結果連客房佈置都沒有 有點小失望 
感覺開業的有點倉促 電話壞了兩天沒有打通 游泳都閉着 地下車庫因為連着寫字樓搞得有點踢踏 
客房服務送個東西要一小時以上 阿姨扣扣搜搜的 要兩瓶水給一瓶 多要一雙拖鞋都不肯 有點無語 但衝著這個開業價格也就忍了吧
早餐很OK 有澳門的檔次 自助餐衹有周四到週日開放 套內的話衹能預約週五六
套餐內容有點雞肋 用餐期間本身就有免費的咖啡 收費的無非就是多了個拉花 本想另一杯晚一點再點 退房後也忘記了 還不如價格貴一點給個mini吧代金券下午茶什麼的
房內有很多細節需要被吐槽 鬧鐘快了一個小時 紙巾很臭 乾濕分離共用一扇透明移門 一個人住還OK 否則真的挺尷尬的
總而言之吧 酒店很漂亮，房間景色也很漂亮，是一個剛開業的酒店，設施設備都很新，酒店大堂的設計據説是參考了杭州的雷峯塔，非常有創意。禮賓部的Charles服務很好。

msg:酒店房間潔具是用科勒的，比較好搞衞生的（見識有限，也就衹認識這幾個衞浴牌而已，僅限於個人觀點），床品就不知道是什麼品牌了，但沒有異味，被單床單枕單表面都是潔白的，沙發和凳子都是皮的，顏色明朗，沒有污漬，桌子都是大理石麪的，有點輕奢的感覺，所以感覺衞生還是不錯的；我們衹在酒店訂了早餐，品種齊全，味道中規中矩；酒店的服務肯定是培訓到位了，大部分工作人員禮貌得體有迴應，雖然也有個別工作人員對着你服務時沒句交待就突然接聽電話，晾你在一邊，跟她説謝謝也像沒聽見似的，還有游泳場買泳帽時，對客人的挑挑撿撿不耐煩，對待客人的求助衹會説這不行那不行，就是不會解決問題，還好都是些小插曲，酒店的處理並沒有讓這些小事情變成客人心中的一根刺，影響到好心情！當然遇到這些小事情作為客人的我自己也要放好心態，畢竟人與人之間打交道，有的有緣分，有的沒緣分，工作人員也是辛苦的，肯定都是盡力了的，但誰都有個心情不好的時候，業務專業能力雙強的不帶到工作中來，不強的多多少少情緒化一點帶到工作中來了，所以總得來説，謝謝我們遇見的所有的酒店工作人員，辛苦啦！

name:F‍e‍n‍g‍g‍e
info:2 Twin Standard
info:Stayed in April 2023
info:Couples
info:5 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted April 3, 2023
msg:看到攜程一系列5星好評，我是非常驚訝的。這家酒店是個不錯，但優缺點確實都非常明顯的酒店。
先説優點吧：
1. 服務是不錯的，能明顯感覺酒店是想要做好的，服務人員態度都很積極，也樂於解決問題。
2. 基礎房設計OK，無論是公務出差還是私人旅行都能兼顧。
3. 整體而言 硬件水平不錯，至少在皇冠假日平均水平之上，可以和某些老洲際相比。
酒店的缺點也很明顯：
1. 酒店現在是試運營，健身房泳池是沒開放的，這點酒店沒有主動告知客户，很不好。
2.酒店房間的味道很大而且空氣凈化器嚴重不足，即使酒店後來提供的空氣凈化器也不是能夠過濾甲醛的。
3. 要想通風衹能開窗，好巧不巧如果你隔壁也開窗的話，你就衹能祈禱隔壁別吵架了。
4.自助餐質量不錯，但7點去後基本沒啥東西，生蠔更是全程沒見過。
總結一下，酒店是個好酒店，但現在正處於磨合期不太適合即可入住。週末998帶雙人自助晚餐但房券可以説是誠意滿滿。建議囤點券三個月後再住吧。
----------------------------------------
